equation EQ_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF.ls ST_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF c PT_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF PT_UNITED_STATES

equation EQ_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF_MD1.ls ST_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF c (PT_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF - PT_UNITED_STATES)

equation EQ_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF_MD2.ls (ST_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF - PT_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF) c PT_UNITED_STATES
EQ_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF_MD2.makeresids RES_MD2_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF
equation EQ_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF_MD3.ls (ST_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF +  PT_UNITED_STATES) c PT_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF
EQ_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF_MD3.makeresids RES_MD3_AFGHANISTAN_ISLAMIC_REPUBLIC_OF

equation EQ_SEYCHELLES_MD1.ls ST_SEYCHELLES c (PT_SEYCHELLES - PT_UNITED_STATES)

EQ_URUGUAY.makeresids RES_URUGUAY
